\'\',\n        Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\') ?? \'\'\n      );\n      const update: Record<string, unknown> = { ai_interpretation: interpretation, strategy_params: params };\n      if (risk.stop_loss_pct !== null) update.stop_loss_pct = risk.stop_loss_pct;\n      if (risk.take_profit_pct !== null) update.take_profit_pct = risk.take_profit_pct;\n      if (risk.position_size_pct !== null) update.position_size_pct = risk.position_size_pct;\n      if (risk.tp1_pct !== null) update.tp1_pct = risk.tp1_pct;\n      if (risk.tp2_pct !== null) update.tp2_pct = risk.tp2_pct;\n      if (risk.tp3_pct !== null) update.tp3_pct = risk.tp3_pct;\n      if (risk.tp1_size_pct !== null) update.tp1_size_pct = risk.tp1_size_pct;\n      if (risk.tp2_size_pct !== null) update.tp2_size_pct = risk.tp2_size_pct;\n      if (risk.tp3_size_pct !== null) update.tp3_size_pct = risk.tp3_size_pct;\n      await supabase.from(\'strategies\').update(update).eq(\'id\', strategyId);\n    }\n\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ interpretation, params, risk }),\n      { headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' } }\n    );\n  } catch (err) {\n    return new Response(\n      JSON.stringify({ error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : \'Analysis failed\' }),\n      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' } }\n    );\n  }\n});\n\n/** Extract numeric parameters from PineScript using regex patterns */\nfunction extractParams(code: string): StrategyParams {\n  const num = (pattern: RegExp, fallback: number) => {\n    const m = code.match(pattern);\n    return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : fallback;\n  };\n\n  const rsi_length = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?RSI/i, 0) ||\n    num(/ta\\.rsi\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/i, 14);\n\n  const overbought = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?overbought/i, 0) ||\n    num(/overbought\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 70);\n\n  const oversold = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?oversold/i, 0) ||\n    num(/oversold\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 30);\n\n  const emaMatches = [...code.matchAll(/ta\\.ema\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/gi)]\n    .map(m => parseInt(m[1], 10))\n    .sort((a, b) => a - b);\n\n  const ema_fast = emaMatches[0] ?? num(/ema_fast\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 20);\n  const ema_slow = emaMatches[1] ?? num(/ema_slow\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 50);\n\n  const symbolHint = code.match(/\\b(BTCUSDT|ETHUSDT|SOLUSDT|BNBUSDT)\\b/i);\n  const symbol = symbolHint ? symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : \'BTCUSDT\';\n\n  const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\\s*[=:]\\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']/i);\n  const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : \'1h\';\n\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const has_stop_loss = lower.includes(\'loss=\') || lower.includes(\'stop_loss\') || lower.includes(\'strategy.exit\');\n  const has_take_profit = lower.includes(\'profit=\') || lower.includes(\'take_profit\');\n  const hasLong = lower.includes(\'strategy.long\');\n  const hasShort = lower.includes(\'strategy.short\');\n  const trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\' = (hasLong && hasShort) ? \'both\' : hasShort ? \'short\' : \'long\';\n\n  return { rsi_length, overbought, oversold, ema_fast, ema_slow, symbol, timeframe, has_stop_loss, has_take_profit, trade_direction };\n}\n\n/** Extract stop-loss, single TP, and multi-TP (TP1/TP2/TP3) from PineScript */\nfunction extractRiskPct(code: string): {\n  stop_loss_pct: number | null;\n  take_profit_pct: number | null;\n  position_size_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;\n} {\n  const flt = (pattern: RegExp) => {\n    const m = code.match(pattern);\n    return m ? parseFloat(m[1]) : null;\n  };\n\n  // ── Stop Loss ──\n  const slInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:stop.?loss|[^"\']*\\bsl\\b)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const stop_loss_pct = slInput ?? (lossTickM ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(lossTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 20) : null);\n\n  // ── Position Size ──\n  const position_size_pct = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:position.?size|size|qty)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // ── Multi-TP: input.float(1.5, "TP1 %") / input.float(3, "TP1") / tp1 = input.float(1.5, "Take Profit 1") ──\n  const tp1Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp1|tp\\s*1|take.?profit\\s*1|target\\s*1)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const tp2Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp2|tp\\s*2|take.?profit\\s*2|target\\s*2)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const tp3Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp3|tp\\s*3|take.?profit\\s*3|target\\s*3)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // ── Multi-TP: strategy.exit("TP1", ..., profit=150, qty_percent=33) ──\n  const exitBlocks = [...code.matchAll(/strategy\\.exit\\s*\\(\\s*["\']([^"\']*?)["\'][^)]*profit\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)[^)]*(?:qty_percent\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?))?/gi)];\n\n  let tp1_exit: number | null = null, tp2_exit: number | null = null, tp3_exit: number | null = null;\n  let tp1s_exit: number | null = null, tp2s_exit: number | null = null, tp3s_exit: number | null = null;\n\n  for (const b of exitBlocks) {\n    const label = b[1].toLowerCase();\n    const pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(b[2]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50);\n    const sz = b[3] ? parseFloat(b[3]) : null;\n    if (label.includes(\'tp1\') || label.includes(\'tp 1\') || label.includes(\'target1\') || label.includes(\'1\')) {\n      if (!tp1_exit) { tp1_exit = pct; tp1s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp2\') || label.includes(\'tp 2\') || label.includes(\'target2\') || label.includes(\'2\')) {\n      if (!tp2_exit) { tp2_exit = pct; tp2s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp3\') || label.includes(\'tp 3\') || label.includes(\'target3\') || label.includes(\'3\')) {\n      if (!tp3_exit) { tp3_exit = pct; tp3s_exit = sz; }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Fallback: single profit= tick\n  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const singleTpInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  const tp1_pct = tp1Input ?? tp1_exit;\n  const tp2_pct = tp2Input ?? tp2_exit;\n  const tp3_pct = tp3Input ?? tp3_exit;\n  const tp1_size_pct = tp1s_exit;\n  const tp2_size_pct = tp2s_exit;\n  const tp3_size_pct = tp3s_exit;\n\n  // single TP fallback (for backward-compat field)\n  const take_profit_pct = tp1_pct ?? singleTpInput ??\n    (profitTickM && !exitBlocks.length ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50) : null);\n\n  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct, tp1_pct, tp2_pct, tp3_pct, tp1_size_pct, tp2_size_pct, tp3_size_pct };\n}\n\nfunction buildInterpretation(code: string, p: StrategyParams, risk: {\n  stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;\n}): string {\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const findings: string[] = [];\n  if (lower.includes(\'rsi\')) findings.push(\'• RSI — momentum oscillator\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'macd\')) findings.push(\'• MACD — trend-following momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema\') || lower.includes(\'sma\')) findings.push(\'• Moving Averages (EMA/SMA) — trend confirmation\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'bollinger\') || lower.includes(\'bb.\')) findings.push(\'• Bollinger Bands — volatility\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'stoch\')) findings.push(\'• Stochastic — momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'atr\')) findings.push(\'• ATR — volatility/stop sizing\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'volume\')) findings.push(\'• Volume — signal confirmation\');\n\n  const linesCount = code.split(\'\\n\').length;\n  const v5 = code.includes(\'@version=5\');\n  const isStrat = lower.includes(\'strategy(\');\n\n  let r = `📊 AI Strategy Analysis\\n\\n`;\n  r += `Type: ${isStrat ? \'Full Strategy\' : \'Indicator\'} | Version: PineScript ${v5 ? \'v5\' : \'v4\'} | Lines: ${linesCount}\\n\\n`;\n  if (findings.length) r += `🔬 Indicators:\\n${findings.join(\'\\n\')}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `⚙️ Extracted Parameters:\\n`;\n  r += `• RSI Length: ${p.rsi_length} | Overbought: ${p.overbought} | Oversold: ${p.oversold}\\n`;\n  r += `• EMA Fast: ${p.ema_fast} | EMA Slow: ${p.ema_slow}\\n`;\n  r += `• Trade Direction: ${p.trade_direction} | Symbol: ${p.symbol}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `🟢 Entry Conditions:\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ta.crossover\')) r += `• RSI crosses above oversold (${p.oversold})\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema_fast\') || p.ema_fast) r += `• EMA${p.ema_fast} > EMA${p.ema_slow} (uptrend filter)\\n`;\n\n  r += `\\n⚙️ Risk Management:\\n`;\n  r += p.has_stop_loss ? `• Stop Loss defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No stop loss detected`;\n  if (risk.stop_loss_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.stop_loss_pct}%)`;\n  r += \'\\n\';\n\n  // Multi-TP summary\n  const hasMultiTp = risk.tp1_pct || risk.tp2_pct || risk.tp3_pct;\n  if (hasMultiTp) {\n    r += `• Multi-Target Take Profits detected:\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp1_pct) r += `  TP1: ${risk.tp1_pct}%${risk.tp1_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp1_size_pct}% of position)` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp2_pct) r += `  TP2: ${risk.tp2_pct}%${risk.tp2_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp2_size_pct}% of position)` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp3_pct) r += `  TP3: ${risk.tp3_pct}%${risk.tp3_size_pct ? ` (${risk.tp3_size_pct}% of position)` : \'\'}\\n`;\n  } else {\n    r += p.has_take_profit ? `• Take Profit defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No take profit detected`;\n    if (risk.take_profit_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.take_profit_pct}%)`;\n    r += \'\\n\';\n  }\n  if (risk.position_size_pct) r += `• Position Size: ${risk.position_size_pct}% of balance\\n`;\n\n  r += `\\n⚡ Bot Integration:\\nWhen activated, the bot fetches live ${p.symbol} klines, computes RSI(${p.rsi_length}) and EMA${p.ema_fast}/EMA${p.ema_slow}, then places a ${p.trade_direction} order on Binance when entry conditions are met.`;\n  return r;\n}\n'}]}

overbought: number;\n  oversold: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  symbol: string;\n  timeframe: string;\n  has_stop_loss: boolean;\n  has_take_profit: boolean;\n  trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\';\n}\n\ninterface OHLCV {\n  close: number;\n  high: number;\n  low: number;\n}\n\ninterface SignalResult {\n  signal: \'BUY\' | \'SELL\' | \'HOLD\';\n  reason: string;\n  rsi: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  price: number;\n}\n\n/* ─── Supabase service client ─── */\nfunction sb() {\n  return createClient(\n    Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_URL\')!,\n    Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\')!,\n  );\n}\n\n/* ─── Binance helpers ─── */\nasync function hmacSha256(secret: string, msg: string): Promise<string> {\n  const enc = new TextEncoder();\n  const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\'raw\', enc.encode(secret), { name: \'HMAC\', hash: \'SHA-256\' }, false, [\'sign\']);\n  const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign(\'HMAC\', key, enc.encode(msg));\n  return Array.from(new Uint8Array(sig)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, \'0\')).join(\'\');\n}\n\nasync function signedPost(base: string, path: string, apiKey: string, secret: string, params: Record<string, string>) {\n  const ts = Date.now().toString();\n  const all = { ...params, recvWindow: RECV_WINDOW, timestamp: ts };\n  const qs = new URLSearchParams(all).toString();\n  const sig = await hmacSha256(secret, qs);\n  const res = await fetch(`${base}${path}?${qs}&signature=${sig}`, {\n    method: \'POST\',\n    headers: { low: parseFloat(c[3] as string),\n  }));\n}\n\n/* ─── Technical Indicators ─── */\nfunction calcRSI(closes: number[], period: number): number {\n  if (closes.length < period + 1) return 50;\n  let gains = 0, losses = 0;\n  for (let i = closes.length - period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    const diff = closes[i] - closes[i - 1];\n    if (diff > 0) gains += diff; else losses -= diff;\n  }\n  const avgGain = gains / period;\n  const avgLoss = losses / period;\n  if (avgLoss === 0) return 100;\n  const rs = avgGain / avgLoss;\n  return +(100 - 100 / (1 + rs)).toFixed(2);\n}\n\nfunction calcEMA(closes: number[], period: number): number {\n  if (closes.length < period) return closes[closes.length - 1];\n  const k = 2 / (period + 1);\n  let ema = closes.slice(0, period).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / period;\n  for (let i = period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    ema = closes[i] * k + ema * (1 - k);\n  }\n  return +ema.toFixed(6);\n}\n\n/* ─── Signal evaluation ─── */\nfunction evaluateSignal(closes: number[], params: StrategyParams): SignalResult {\n  const rsi = calcRSI(closes, params.rsi_length);\n  const emaF = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_fast);\n  const emaS = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_slow);\n  const price = closes[closes.length - 1];\n\n  const prevRsi = calcRSI(closes.slice(0, -1), params.rsi_length);\n  const bullishCross = prevRsi <= params.oversold && rsi > params.oversold;\n  const bearishCross = prevRsi >= params.overbought && rsi < params.overbought;\n  const uptrend = emaF > emaS;\n  const downtrend = emaF < emaS;\n\n  const canLong = params.trade_direction === \'long\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n  const canShort = params.trade_direction === \'short\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n\n  if (canLong && bullishCross && uptrend) {\n    return { signal: \'BUY\', reason: `RSI crossed above oversold (${params.oversold}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} > EMA${params.ema_slow} uptrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n  if (canShort && bearishCross && downtrend) {\n    return { signal: \'SELL\', reason: `RSI crossed below overbought (${params.overbought}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} < EMA${params.ema_slow} downtrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n\n  return {\n    signal: \'HOLD\',\n    reason: `RSI=${rsi} | EMA${params.ema_fast}=${emaF.toFixed(2)} | EMA${params.ema_slow}=${emaS.toFixed(2)} — no entry condition met`,\n    rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price,\n  };\n}\n\n/* ─── Minimum notional helper (USDT pairs) ─── */\nfunction calcQuantity(price: number, positionPct: number, _symbol: string): number {\n  const budget = 1000 * (positionPct / 100); // assume $1000 base (real: fetch account balance)\n  const qty = budget / price;\n  // round to reasonable precision\n  if (price > 1000) return +qty.toFixed(5);\n  if (price > 1) return +qty.toFixed(3);\n  return +qty.toFixed(1);\n}\n\nconst TF_INTERVAL: Record<string, string> = {\n  \'1m\': \'1m\', \'5m\': \'5m\', \'15m\': \'15m\', \'30m\': \'30m\',\n  \'1h\': \'1h\', \'4h\': \'4h\', \'1d\': \'1d\',\n};\n\n/* ─── Main handler ─── */\nDeno.serve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === \'OPTIONS\') return new Response(\'ok\', { headers: corsHeaders });\n\n  const authHeader = try {\n    const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split(\'.\')[1]));\n    userId = payload.sub;\n  } catch {\n    return json({ error: \'Invalid token\' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  let body: { strategyId: string };\n  try { body = await req.json(); } catch { return json({ error: \'Invalid JSON\' }, 400); }\n  if (!body.strategyId) return json({ error: \'strategyId is required\' }, 400);\n\n  const client = sb();\n\n  /* 1. Load strategy */\n  const { data: strategy, error: stratErr } = await client\n    .from(\'strategies\')\n    .select(\'*\')\n    .eq(\'id\', body.strategyId)\n    .eq(\'user_id\', userId)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (stratErr || !strategy) return json({ error: \'Strategy not found\' }, 404);\n\n  const params = strategy.strategy_params as StrategyParams | null;\n  if (!params) return json({ error: \'Strategy not analyzed yet. New String: ```
  const runAnalyze = async (strategy: Strategy, showToast = true) => {
    setInterpreting(strategy.id);
    const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('analyze-pinescript', {
      body: { strategyId: strategy.id, code: strategy.pinescript_code },
      method: 'POST',
    });
    if (error || !data?.interpretation) {
      const fallback = `📊 Strategy Analysis: "${strategy.name}"\n\n` +
        `• Entry signals detected in PineScript code\n` +
        `• Uses RSI momentum indicators\n` +
        `• Trend confirmation via EMA crossovers\n` +
        `• Risk management: stop loss and take profit defined\n\n` +
        `⚡ Bot will monitor for entry conditions matching this strategy and execute trades via your Binance API.`;
      await updateStrategy(strategy.id, { ai_interpretation: fallback });
      if (showToast) toast.success('Strategy analyzed (demo mode)');
    } else {
      if (showToast) {
        const risk = data.risk as { tp1_pct?: number; tp2_pct?: number; tp3_pct?: number; stop_loss_pct?: number } | undefined;
        const extracted: string[] = [];
        if (risk?.stop_loss_pct) extracted.push(`SL: ${risk.stop_loss_pct}%`);
        if (risk?.tp1_pct) extracted.push(`TP1: ${risk.tp1_pct}%`);
        if (risk?.tp2_pct) extracted.push(`TP2: ${risk.tp2_pct}%`);
        if (risk?.tp3_pct) extracted.push(`TP3: ${risk.tp3_pct}%`);
        const hint = extracted.length ? ` — Extracted: ${extracted.join(', ')}` : '';
        toast.success(`Strategy analyzed by AI!${hint}`, { icon: '🤖', duration: 6000 });
      }
    }
    // Reload and auto-sync Risk Settings panel with extracted values
    const updated = await getStrategies();
    setStrategies(updated);
    const fresh = updated.find(s => s.id === strategy.id) ?? null;
    if (fresh) {
      // Always re-sync the panel — whether this is the selected strategy or auto-analyze on create
      if (selectedStrategy?.id === strategy.id || !showToast) {
        handleSelectStrategy(fresh);
      }
    }
    setInterpreting(null);
  };
```

  // Sync risk form from a strategy object
  const syncRiskForm = useCallback((s: Strategy) => {

      stop_loss_pct: s.stop_loss_pct != null ? String(s.stop_loss_pct) : '',
      take_profit_pct: s.take_profit_pct != null ? String(s.take_profit_pct) : '',

  const runAnalyze = async (strategy: Strategy, showToast = true) => {
    setInterpreting(strategy.id);
    const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('analyze-pinescript', {
      body: { strategyId: strategy.id, code: strategy.pinescript_code },
      method: 'POST',

New String: ```
  // Fallback: single profit= tick
  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\s*=\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)/i);
  const singleTpInput = flt(/input(?:\.float|\.int)?\s*\(\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*,\s*["'][^"']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"']*["']/i);

  // Resolve single TP baseline
  const singleTpRaw = singleTpInput ??
    (profitTickM && !exitBlocks.length ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50) : null);

  // ── Smart inference: if no explicit TP1/TP2/TP3, derive from single TP or SL ──
  // Priority: explicit extraction > smart inference
  let tp1_pct = tp1Input ?? tp1_exit;
  let tp2_pct = tp2Input ?? tp2_exit;
  let tp3_pct = tp3Input ?? tp3_exit;
  let tp1_size_pct = tp1s_exit;
  let tp2_size_pct = tp2s_exit;
  let tp3_size_pct = tp3s_exit;

  if (!tp1_pct && !tp2_pct && !tp3_pct) {
    if (singleTpRaw) {
      // Split single TP into 3 scaled levels: 1x, 1.5x, 2.5x
      tp1_pct = +singleTpRaw.toFixed(2);
      tp2_pct = +(singleTpRaw * 1.5).toFixed(2);
      tp3_pct = +(singleTpRaw * 2.5).toFixed(2);
    } else if (stop_loss_pct) {
      // No TP at all — infer from R:R ratios (1:1.5, 1:2.5, 1:4)
      tp1_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 1.5).toFixed(2);
      tp2_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 2.5).toFixed(2);
      tp3_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 4.0).toFixed(2);
    }
  }

  // Smart default sizes if not extracted: close 50% at TP1, 30% at TP2, 20% at TP3
  if (tp1_pct && !tp1_size_pct) tp1_size_pct = 50;
  if (tp2_pct && !tp2_size_pct) tp2_size_pct = 30;
  if (tp3_pct && !tp3_size_pct) tp3_size_pct = 20;

  // single TP fallback (for backward-compat field)
  const take_profit_pct = singleTpRaw ?? tp1_pct;

  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct, tp1_pct, tp2_pct, tp3_pct, tp1_size_pct, tp2_size_pct, tp3_size_pct };
}

const SAMPLE_PINESCRIPT = `//@version=5
strategy("My RSI + EMA Strategy", overlay=true, default_qty_type=strategy.percent_of_equity, default_qty_value=10)

// ── Inputs ──
rsiLen     = input.int(14,   "RSI Length")
overbought = input.int(70,   "Overbought Level")
oversold   = input.int(30,   "Oversold Level")
slPct      = input.float(1.5, "Stop Loss %",      step=0.1)
tp1Pct     = input.float(1.5, "TP1 % (50% qty)",  step=0.1)
tp2Pct     = input.float(3.0, "TP2 % (30% qty)",  step=0.1)
tp3Pct     = input.float(5.0, "TP3 % (20% qty)",  step=0.1)

// ── Indicators ──
rsi      = ta.rsi(close, rsiLen)
ema_fast = ta.ema(close, 20)
ema_slow = ta.ema(close, 50)

// ── Conditions ──
longCondition  = ta.crossover(rsi, oversold)  and ema_fast > ema_slow
shortCondition = ta.crossunder(rsi, overbought) and ema_fast < ema_slow

// ── Entries ──
if longCondition
    strategy.entry("Long", strategy.long)
if shortCondition
    strategy.entry("Short", strategy.short)

// ── Multi-Target Exits ──
strategy.exit("TP1-L", from_entry="Long",  profit=tp1Pct*100, loss=slPct*100, qty_percent=50)
strategy.exit("TP2-L", from_entry="Long",  profit=tp2Pct*100, loss=slPct*100, qty_percent=30)
strategy.exit("TP3-L", from_entry="Long",  profit=tp3Pct*100, loss=slPct*100, qty_percent=20)
strategy.exit("TP1-S", from_entry="Short", profit=tp1Pct*100, loss=slPct*100, qty_percent=50)
strategy.exit("TP2-S", from_entry="Short", profit=tp2Pct*100, loss=slPct*100, qty_percent=30)
strategy.exit("TP3-S", from_entry="Short", profit=tp3Pct*100, loss=slPct*100, qty_percent=20)`;

parseInt(m[1], 10) : fallback;\n  };\n\n  const rsi_length = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?RSI/i, 0) ||\n    num(/ta\\.rsi\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/i, 14);\n\n  const overbought = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?overbought/i, 0) ||\n    num(/overbought\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 70);\n\n  const oversold = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?oversold/i, 0) ||\n    num(/oversold\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 30);\n\n  const emaMatches = [...code.matchAll(/ta\\.ema\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/gi)]\n    .map(m => parseInt(m[1], 10))\n    .sort((a, b) => a - b);\n\n  const ema_fast = emaMatches[0] ?? num(/ema_fast\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 20);\n  const ema_slow = emaMatches[1] ?? num(/ema_slow\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 50);\n\n  const symbolHint = code.match(/\\b(BTCUSDT|ETHUSDT|SOLUSDT|BNBUSDT)\\b/i);\n  const symbol = symbolHint ? symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : \'BTCUSDT\';\n\n  const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\\s*[=:]\\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']/i);\n  const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : \'1h\';\n\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const has_stop_loss = lower.includes(\'loss=\') || lower.includes(\'stop_loss\') || lower.includes(\'strategy.exit\');\n  const has_take_profit = lower.includes(\'profit=\') || lower.includes(\'take_profit\');\n  const hasLong = lower.includes(\'strategy.long\');\n  const hasShort = lower.includes(\'strategy.short\');\n  const trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\' = (hasLong && hasShort) ? parseFloat(m[1]) : null;\n  };\n\n  // ── Stop Loss ──\n  const slInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:stop.?loss|[^"\']*\\bsl\\b)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const stop_loss_pct = slInput ?? parseFloat(b[3]) : null;\n    if (label.includes(\'tp1\') || label.includes(\'tp 1\') || label.includes(\'target1\') || label.includes(\'1\')) {\n      if (!tp1_exit) { tp1_exit = pct; tp1s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp2\') || label.includes(\'tp 2\') || label.includes(\'target2\') || label.includes(\'2\')) {\n      if (!tp2_exit) { tp2_exit = pct; tp2s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp3\') || label.includes(\'tp 3\') || label.includes(\'target3\') || label.includes(\'3\')) {\n      if (!tp3_exit) { tp3_exit = pct; tp3s_exit = sz; }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Fallback: single profit= tick\n  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const singleTpInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // Resolve single TP baseline\n  const singleTpRaw = singleTpInput ??\n    (profitTickM && !exitBlocks.length ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50) : null);\n\n  // ── Smart inference: if no explicit TP1/TP2/TP3, derive from single TP or SL ──\n  // Priority: explicit extraction > smart inference\n  let tp1_pct = tp1Input ?? tp1_exit;\n  let tp2_pct = tp2Input ?? tp2_exit;\n  let tp3_pct = tp3Input ?? tp3_exit;\n  let tp1_size_pct = tp1s_exit;\n  let tp2_size_pct = tp2s_exit;\n  let tp3_size_pct = tp3s_exit;\n\n  if (!tp1_pct && !tp2_pct && !tp3_pct) {\n    if (singleTpRaw) {\n      // Split single TP into 3 scaled levels: 1x, 1.5x, 2.5x\n      tp1_pct = +singleTpRaw.toFixed(2);\n      tp2_pct = +(singleTpRaw * 1.5).toFixed(2);\n      tp3_pct = +(singleTpRaw * 2.5).toFixed(2);\n    } else if (stop_loss_pct) {\n      // No TP at all — infer from R:R ratios (1:1.5, 1:2.5, 1:4)\n      tp1_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 1.5).toFixed(2);\n      tp2_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 2.5).toFixed(2);\n      tp3_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 4.0).toFixed(2);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Smart default sizes if not extracted: close 50% at TP1, 30% at TP2, 20% at TP3\n  if (tp1_pct && !tp1_size_pct) tp1_size_pct = 50;\n  if (tp2_pct && !tp2_size_pct) tp2_size_pct = 30;\n  if (tp3_pct && !tp3_size_pct) tp3_size_pct = 20;\n\n  // single TP fallback (for backward-compat field)\n  const take_profit_pct = singleTpRaw ?? tp1_pct;\n\n  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct, tp1_pct, tp2_pct, tp3_pct, tp1_size_pct, tp2_size_pct, tp3_size_pct };\n}\n\nfunction buildInterpretation(code: string, p: StrategyParams, risk: {\n  stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;\n}): string {\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const findings: string[] = [];\n  if (lower.includes(\'rsi\')) findings.push(\'• RSI — momentum oscillator\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'macd\')) findings.push(\'• MACD — trend-following momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema\') || lower.includes(\'sma\')) findings.push(\'• Moving Averages (EMA/SMA) — trend confirmation\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'bollinger\') || lower.includes(\'bb.\')) findings.push(\'• Bollinger Bands — volatility\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'stoch\')) findings.push(\'• Stochastic — momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'atr\')) findings.push(\'• ATR — volatility/stop sizing\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'volume\')) findings.push(\'• Volume — signal confirmation\');\n\n  const linesCount = code.split(\'\\n\').length;\n  const v5 = code.includes(\'@version=5\');\n  const isStrat = lower.includes(\'strategy(\');\n\n  let r = `📊 AI Strategy Analysis\\n\\n`;\n  r += `Type: ${isStrat ? \'Full Strategy\' : \'Indicator\'} | Version: PineScript ${v5 ? \'v5\' : \'v4\'} | Lines: ${linesCount}\\n\\n`;\n  if (findings.length) r += `🔬 Indicators:\\n${findings.join(\'\\n\')}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `⚙️ Extracted Parameters:\\n`;\n  r += `• RSI Length: ${p.rsi_length} | Overbought: ${p.overbought} | Oversold: ${p.oversold}\\n`;\n  r += `• EMA Fast: ${p.ema_fast} | EMA Slow: ${p.ema_slow}\\n`;\n  r += `• Trade Direction: ${p.trade_direction} | Symbol: ${p.symbol}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `🟢 Entry Conditions:\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ta.crossover\')) r += `• RSI crosses above oversold (${p.oversold})\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema_fast\') || p.ema_fast) r += `• EMA${p.ema_fast} > EMA${p.ema_slow} (uptrend filter)\\n`;\n\n  r += `\\n⚙️ Risk Management:\\n`;\n  r += p.has_stop_loss ? \' (AI-inferred from strategy)\' : \' (extracted from PineScript)\'}:\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp1_pct) r += `  TP1: ${risk.tp1_pct}%${risk.tp1_size_pct ? ` → close ${risk.tp1_size_pct}% of position` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp2_pct) r += `  TP2: ${risk.tp2_pct}%${risk.tp2_size_pct ?    224   const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);

err.message : \'Analysis failed\' }),\n      { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' } }\n    );\n  }\n});\n\n/** Extract numeric parameters from PineScript using regex patterns */\nfunction extractParams(code: string): StrategyParams {\n  const num = (pattern: RegExp, fallback: number) => {\n    const m = code.match(pattern);\n    return m ? parseInt(m[1], 10) : fallback;\n  };\n\n  const rsi_length = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?RSI/i, 0) ||\n    num(/ta\\.rsi\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/i, 14);\n\n  const overbought = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?overbought/i, 0) ||\n    num(/overbought\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 70);\n\n  const oversold = num(/input\\.int\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+)\\s*,\\s*["\']?oversold/i, 0) ||\n    num(/oversold\\s*=\\s*(\\d+)/i, 30);\n\n  const emaMatches = [...code.matchAll(/ta\\.ema\\s*\\(\\s*\\w+\\s*,\\s*(\\d+)\\s*\\)/gi)]\n    .map(m => parseInt(m[1], 10))\n    .sort((a, b) => a - b);\n\n  const ema_fast = emaMatches[0] ?? num(/ema_fast\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 20);\n  const ema_slow = emaMatches[1] ?? num(/ema_slow\\s*=.*?(\\d+)/i, 50);\n\n  const symbolHint = code.match(/\\b(BTCUSDT|ETHUSDT|SOLUSDT|BNBUSDT)\\b/i);\n  const symbol = symbolHint ? symbolHint[1].toUpperCase() : \'BTCUSDT\';\n\n  const tfMatch = code.match(/timeframe\\s*[=:]\\s*["\']([^"\']+)["\']/i);\n  const timeframe = tfMatch ? tfMatch[1] : \'1h\';\n\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const has_stop_loss = lower.includes(\'loss=\') || lower.includes(\'stop_loss\') || lower.includes(\'strategy.exit\');\n  const has_take_profit = lower.includes(\'profit=\') || lower.includes(\'take_profit\');\n  const hasLong = lower.includes(\'strategy.long\');\n  const hasShort = lower.includes(\'strategy.short\');\n  const trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\' = (hasLong && hasShort) ? \'both\' : hasShort ? \'short\' : \'long\';\n\n  return { rsi_length, overbought, oversold, ema_fast, ema_slow, symbol, timeframe, has_stop_loss, has_take_profit, trade_direction };\n}\n\n/** Extract stop-loss, single TP, and multi-TP (TP1/TP2/TP3) from PineScript */\nfunction extractRiskPct(code: string): {\n  stop_loss_pct: number | null;\n  take_profit_pct: number | null;\n  position_size_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;\n} {\n  const flt = (pattern: RegExp) => {\n    const m = code.match(pattern);\n    return m ? parseFloat(m[1]) : null;\n  };\n\n  // ── Stop Loss ──\n  const slInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:stop.?loss|[^"\']*\\bsl\\b)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const lossTickM = code.match(/loss\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const stop_loss_pct = slInput ?? (lossTickM ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(lossTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 20) : null);\n\n  // ── Position Size ──\n  const position_size_pct = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:position.?size|size|qty)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // ── Multi-TP: input.float(1.5, "TP1 %") / input.float(3, "TP1") / tp1 = input.float(1.5, "Take Profit 1") ──\n  const tp1Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp1|tp\\s*1|take.?profit\\s*1|target\\s*1)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const tp2Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp2|tp\\s*2|take.?profit\\s*2|target\\s*2)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n  const tp3Input = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:tp3|tp\\s*3|take.?profit\\s*3|target\\s*3)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // ── Multi-TP: strategy.exit("TP1", ..., profit=150, qty_percent=33) ──\n  const exitBlocks = [...code.matchAll(/strategy\\.exit\\s*\\(\\s*["\']([^"\']*?)["\'][^)]*profit\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)[^)]*(?:qty_percent\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?))?/gi)];\n\n  let tp1_exit: number | null = null, tp2_exit: number | null = null, tp3_exit: number | null = null;\n  let tp1s_exit: number | null = null, tp2s_exit: number | null = null, tp3s_exit: number | null = null;\n\n  for (const b of exitBlocks) {\n    const label = b[1].toLowerCase();\n    const pct = Math.min(+(parseFloat(b[2]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50);\n    const sz = b[3] ? parseFloat(b[3]) : null;\n    if (label.includes(\'tp1\') || label.includes(\'tp 1\') || label.includes(\'target1\') || label.includes(\'1\')) {\n      if (!tp1_exit) { tp1_exit = pct; tp1s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp2\') || label.includes(\'tp 2\') || label.includes(\'target2\') || label.includes(\'2\')) {\n      if (!tp2_exit) { tp2_exit = pct; tp2s_exit = sz; }\n    } else if (label.includes(\'tp3\') || label.includes(\'tp 3\') || label.includes(\'target3\') || label.includes(\'3\')) {\n      if (!tp3_exit) { tp3_exit = pct; tp3s_exit = sz; }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Fallback: single profit= tick\n  const profitTickM = code.match(/profit\\s*=\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)/i);\n  const singleTpInput = flt(/input(?:\\.float|\\.int)?\\s*\\(\\s*(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?)\\s*,\\s*["\'][^"\']*(?:take.?profit|tp|target)[^"\']*["\']/i);\n\n  // Resolve single TP baseline\n  const singleTpRaw = singleTpInput ??\n    (profitTickM && !exitBlocks.length ? Math.min(+(parseFloat(profitTickM[1]) * 0.01).toFixed(2), 50) : null);\n\n  // ── Smart inference: if no explicit TP1/TP2/TP3, derive from single TP or SL ──\n  // Priority: explicit extraction > smart inference\n  let tp1_pct = tp1Input ?? tp1_exit;\n  let tp2_pct = tp2Input ?? tp2_exit;\n  let tp3_pct = tp3Input ?? tp3_exit;\n  let tp1_size_pct = tp1s_exit;\n  let tp2_size_pct = tp2s_exit;\n  let tp3_size_pct = tp3s_exit;\n\n  if (!tp1_pct && !tp2_pct && !tp3_pct) {\n    if (singleTpRaw) {\n      // Split single TP into 3 scaled levels: 1x, 1.5x, 2.5x\n      tp1_pct = +singleTpRaw.toFixed(2);\n      tp2_pct = +(singleTpRaw * 1.5).toFixed(2);\n      tp3_pct = +(singleTpRaw * 2.5).toFixed(2);\n    } else if (stop_loss_pct) {\n      // No TP at all — infer from R:R ratios (1:1.5, 1:2.5, 1:4)\n      tp1_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 1.5).toFixed(2);\n      tp2_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 2.5).toFixed(2);\n      tp3_pct = +(stop_loss_pct * 4.0).toFixed(2);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Smart default sizes if not extracted: close 50% at TP1, 30% at TP2, 20% at TP3\n  if (tp1_pct && !tp1_size_pct) tp1_size_pct = 50;\n  if (tp2_pct && !tp2_size_pct) tp2_size_pct = 30;\n  if (tp3_pct && !tp3_size_pct) tp3_size_pct = 20;\n\n  // single TP fallback (for backward-compat field)\n  const take_profit_pct = singleTpRaw ?? tp1_pct;\n\n  return { stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, position_size_pct, tp1_pct, tp2_pct, tp3_pct, tp1_size_pct, tp2_size_pct, tp3_size_pct };\n}\n\nfunction buildInterpretation(code: string, p: StrategyParams, risk: {\n  stop_loss_pct: number | null; take_profit_pct: number | null; position_size_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_pct: number | null; tp2_pct: number | null; tp3_pct: number | null;\n  tp1_size_pct: number | null; tp2_size_pct: number | null; tp3_size_pct: number | null;\n}): string {\n  const lower = code.toLowerCase();\n  const findings: string[] = [];\n  if (lower.includes(\'rsi\')) findings.push(\'• RSI — momentum oscillator\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'macd\')) findings.push(\'• MACD — trend-following momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema\') || lower.includes(\'sma\')) findings.push(\'• Moving Averages (EMA/SMA) — trend confirmation\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'bollinger\') || lower.includes(\'bb.\')) findings.push(\'• Bollinger Bands — volatility\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'stoch\')) findings.push(\'• Stochastic — momentum\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'atr\')) findings.push(\'• ATR — volatility/stop sizing\');\n  if (lower.includes(\'volume\')) findings.push(\'• Volume — signal confirmation\');\n\n  const linesCount = code.split(\'\\n\').length;\n  const v5 = code.includes(\'@version=5\');\n  const isStrat = lower.includes(\'strategy(\');\n\n  let r = `📊 AI Strategy Analysis\\n\\n`;\n  r += `Type: ${isStrat ? \'Full Strategy\' : \'Indicator\'} | Version: PineScript ${v5 ? \'v5\' : \'v4\'} | Lines: ${linesCount}\\n\\n`;\n  if (findings.length) r += `🔬 Indicators:\\n${findings.join(\'\\n\')}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `⚙️ Extracted Parameters:\\n`;\n  r += `• RSI Length: ${p.rsi_length} | Overbought: ${p.overbought} | Oversold: ${p.oversold}\\n`;\n  r += `• EMA Fast: ${p.ema_fast} | EMA Slow: ${p.ema_slow}\\n`;\n  r += `• Trade Direction: ${p.trade_direction} | Symbol: ${p.symbol}\\n\\n`;\n\n  r += `🟢 Entry Conditions:\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ta.crossover\')) r += `• RSI crosses above oversold (${p.oversold})\\n`;\n  if (lower.includes(\'ema_fast\') || p.ema_fast) r += `• EMA${p.ema_fast} > EMA${p.ema_slow} (uptrend filter)\\n`;\n\n  r += `\\n⚙️ Risk Management:\\n`;\n  r += p.has_stop_loss ? `• Stop Loss defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No stop loss detected`;\n  if (risk.stop_loss_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.stop_loss_pct}%)`;\n  r += \'\\n\';\n\n  // Multi-TP summary\n  const hasMultiTp = risk.tp1_pct || risk.tp2_pct || risk.tp3_pct;\n  const isInferred = !code.match(/tp1|tp\\s*1|take.?profit\\s*1|target\\s*1/i) && hasMultiTp;\n  if (hasMultiTp) {\n    r += `• Take Profit Levels${isInferred ? \' (AI-inferred from strategy)\' : \' (extracted from PineScript)\'}:\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp1_pct) r += `  TP1: ${risk.tp1_pct}%${risk.tp1_size_pct ? ` → close ${risk.tp1_size_pct}% of position` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp2_pct) r += `  TP2: ${risk.tp2_pct}%${risk.tp2_size_pct ? ` → close ${risk.tp2_size_pct}% of position` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (risk.tp3_pct) r += `  TP3: ${risk.tp3_pct}%${risk.tp3_size_pct ? ` → close ${risk.tp3_size_pct}% of position` : \'\'}\\n`;\n    if (isInferred) r += `  ℹ️ Levels auto-calculated — edit in Risk Settings panel before executing.\\n`;\n  } else {\n    r += p.has_take_profit ? `• Take Profit defined ✓` : `• ⚠️ No take profit detected`;\n    if (risk.take_profit_pct) r += ` (≈ ${risk.take_profit_pct}%)`;\n    r += \'\\n\';\n  }\n  if (risk.position_size_pct) r += `• Position Size: ${risk.position_size_pct}% of balance\\n`;\n\n  r += `\\n⚡ Bot Integration:\\nWhen activated, the bot fetches live ${p.symbol} klines, computes RSI(${p.rsi_length}) and EMA${p.ema_fast}/EMA${p.ema_slow}, then places a ${p.trade_direction} order on Binance when entry conditions are met.`;\n  return r;\n}\n'}]}

\'Access-Control-Allow-Origin\': \'*\',\n  \'Access-Control-Allow-Headers\': \'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type\',\n};\n\nconst BINANCE_BASE_REAL = \'https://api.binance.com\';\nconst BINANCE_BASE_TEST = \'https://testnet.binance.vision\';\nconst RECV_WINDOW = \'5000\';\n\n/* ─── Types ─── */\ninterface StrategyParams {\n  rsi_length: number;\n  overbought: number;\n  oversold: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  symbol: string;\n  timeframe: string;\n  has_stop_loss: boolean;\n  has_take_profit: boolean;\n  trade_direction: \'long\' | \'short\' | \'both\';\n}\n\ninterface OHLCV {\n  close: number;\n  high: number;\n  low: number;\n}\n\ninterface SignalResult {\n  signal: \'BUY\' | \'SELL\' | \'HOLD\';\n  reason: string;\n  rsi: number;\n  ema_fast: number;\n  ema_slow: number;\n  price: number;\n}\n\n/* ─── Supabase service client ─── */\nfunction sb() {\n  return createClient(\n    Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_URL\')!,\n    Deno.env.get(\'SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY\')!,\n  );\n}\n\n/* ─── Binance helpers ─── */\nasync function hmacSha256(secret: string, msg: string): Promise<string> {\n  const enc = new TextEncoder();\n  const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey(\'raw\', enc.encode(secret), { name: \'HMAC\', hash: \'SHA-256\' }, false, [\'sign\']);\n  const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign(\'HMAC\', key, enc.encode(msg));\n  return Array.from(new Uint8Array(sig)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, \'0\')).join(\'\');\n}\n\nasync function signedPost(base: string, path: string, apiKey: string, secret: string, params: Record<string, string>) {\n  const ts = Date.now().toString();\n  const all = { ...params, recvWindow: RECV_WINDOW, timestamp: ts };\n  const qs = new URLSearchParams(all).toString();\n  const sig = await hmacSha256(secret, qs);\n  const res = await fetch(`${base}${path}?${qs}&signature=${sig}`, {\n    method: \'POST\',\n    headers: { \'X-MBX-APIKEY\': apiKey, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n  });\n  const json = await res.json();\n  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(json.msg || `HTTP ${res.status}`);\n  return json;\n}\n\nasync function fetchKlines(base: string, symbol: string, interval: string, limit: number): Promise<OHLCV[]> {\n  const url = `${base}/api/v3/klines?symbol=${symbol.toUpperCase()}&interval=${interval}&limit=${limit}`;\n  const res = await fetch(url, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(10_000) });\n  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Klines fetch failed: ${res.status}`);\n  const raw: unknown[][] = await res.json();\n  return raw.map(c => ({\n    close: parseFloat(c[4] as string),\n    high: parseFloat(c[2] as string),\n    low: parseFloat(c[3] as string),\n  }));\n}\n\n/* ─── Technical Indicators ─── */\nfunction calcRSI(closes: number[], period: number): number {\n  if (closes.length < period + 1) return 50;\n  let gains = 0, losses = 0;\n  for (let i = closes.length - period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    const diff = closes[i] - closes[i - 1];\n    if (diff > 0) gains += diff; else losses -= diff;\n  }\n  const avgGain = gains / period;\n  const avgLoss = losses / period;\n  if (avgLoss === 0) return 100;\n  const rs = avgGain / avgLoss;\n  return +(100 - 100 / (1 + rs)).toFixed(2);\n}\n\nfunction calcEMA(closes: number[], period: number): number {\n  if (closes.length < period) return closes[closes.length - 1];\n  const k = 2 / (period + 1);\n  let ema = closes.slice(0, period).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / period;\n  for (let i = period; i < closes.length; i++) {\n    ema = closes[i] * k + ema * (1 - k);\n  }\n  return +ema.toFixed(6);\n}\n\n/* ─── Signal evaluation ─── */\nfunction evaluateSignal(closes: number[], params: StrategyParams): SignalResult {\n  const rsi = calcRSI(closes, params.rsi_length);\n  const emaF = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_fast);\n  const emaS = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_slow);\n  const price = closes[closes.length - 1];\n\n  const prevRsi = calcRSI(closes.slice(0, -1), params.rsi_length);\n  const bullishCross = prevRsi <= params.oversold && rsi > params.oversold;\n  const bearishCross = prevRsi >= params.overbought && rsi < params.overbought;\n  const uptrend = emaF > emaS;\n  const downtrend = emaF < emaS;\n\n  const canLong = params.trade_direction === \'long\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n  const canShort = params.trade_direction === \'short\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n\n  if (canLong && bullishCross && uptrend) {\n    return { signal: \'BUY\', reason: `RSI crossed above oversold (${params.oversold}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} > EMA${params.ema_slow} uptrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n  if (canShort && bearishCross && downtrend) {\n    return { signal: \'SELL\', reason: `RSI crossed below overbought (${params.overbought}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} < EMA${params.ema_slow} downtrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n\n  return {\n    signal: \'HOLD\',\n    reason: `RSI=${rsi} | EMA${params.ema_fast}=${emaF.toFixed(2)} | EMA${params.ema_slow}=${emaS.toFixed(2)} — no entry condition met`,\n    rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price,\n  };\n}\n\n/* ─── Minimum notional helper (USDT pairs) ─── */\nfunction calcQuantity(price: number, positionPct: number, _symbol: string): number {\n  const budget = 1000 * (positionPct / 100); // assume $1000 base (real: fetch account balance)\n  const qty = budget / price;\n  // round to reasonable precision\n  if (price > 1000) return +qty.toFixed(5);\n  if (price > 1) return +qty.toFixed(3);\n  return +qty.toFixed(1);\n}\n\nconst TF_INTERVAL: Record<string, string> = {\n  \'1m\': \'1m\', \'5m\': \'5m\', \'15m\': \'15m\', \'30m\': \'30m\',\n  \'1h\': \'1h\', \'4h\': \'4h\', \'1d\': \'1d\',\n};\n\n/* ─── Main handler ─── */\nDeno.serve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === \'OPTIONS\') return new Response(\'ok\', { headers: corsHeaders });\n\n  const authHeader = req.headers.get(\'authorization\') || \'\';\n  const token = authHeader.replace(\'Bearer \', \'\');\n  if (!token) return json({ error: \'Missing authorization\' }, 401);\n\n  let userId = \'\';\n  try {\n    const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split(\'.\')[1]));\n    userId = payload.sub;\n  } catch {\n    return json({ error: \'Invalid token\' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  let body: { strategyId: string };\n  try { body = await req.json(); } catch { return json({ error: \'Invalid JSON\' }, 400); }\n  if (!body.strategyId) return json({ error: \'strategyId is required\' }, 400);\n\n  const client = sb();\n\n  /* 1. Load strategy */\n  const { data: strategy, error: stratErr } = await client\n    .from(\'strategies\')\n    .select(\'*\')\n    .eq(\'id\', body.strategyId)\n    .eq(\'user_id\', userId)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (stratErr || !strategy) return json({ error: \'Strategy not found\' }, 404);\n\n  const params = strategy.strategy_params as StrategyParams | null;\n  if (!params) return json({ error: \'Strategy not analyzed yet. Click "AI Analyze" first.\' }, 400);\n\n  /* 2. Load user settings (API keys + risk params + testnet flag) */\n  const { data: settings } = await client\n    .from(\'user_settings\')\n    .select(\'binance_api_key, binance_api_secret, use_testnet, bot_enabled, position_size_pct, stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, min_confidence\')\n    .eq(\'user_id\', userId)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (!settings?.binance_api_key || !settings?.binance_api_secret) {\n    return json({ error: \'Binance API keys not configured in Settings.\' }, 400);\n  }\n\n  const useTestnet: boolean = settings.use_testnet ?? true;\n  const base = useTestnet ? BINANCE_BASE_TEST : BINANCE_BASE_REAL;\n\n  // Priority: per-strategy values > global user_settings fallback\n  const effectiveSL: number = (strategy.stop_loss_pct ?? settings.stop_loss_pct ?? 2);\n  const effectiveTP: number = (strategy.tp1_pct ?? strategy.take_profit_pct ?? settings.take_profit_pct ?? 4);\n  const effectiveSize: number = (strategy.position_size_pct ?? settings.position_size_pct ?? 5);\n  // Multi-TP levels (null = not configured)\n  const tp1: number | null = strategy.tp1_pct ?? null;\n  const tp2: number | null = strategy.tp2_pct ?? null;\n  const tp3: number | null = strategy.tp3_pct ?? null;\n  const tp1Size: number = strategy.tp1_size_pct ?? 33;\n  const tp2Size: number = strategy.tp2_size_pct ?? 33;\n  const tp3Size: number = strategy.tp3_size_pct ?? 34;\n\n  /* 3. Fetch live klines — strategy.timeframe top-level takes priority over strategy_params.timeframe */\n  const effectiveTF: string = (strategy.timeframe ?? params.timeframe ?? \'1h\');\n  const interval = TF_INTERVAL[effectiveTF] ?? \'1h\';\n  const klineLimit = Math.max(params.rsi_length + 10, params.ema_slow + 10, 60);\n  let candles: OHLCV[];\n  try {\n    candles = await fetchKlines(base, params.symbol, interval, klineLimit);\n  } catch (e: unknown) {\n    return json({ error: `Binance klines error: ${(e as Error).message}` }, 502);\n  }\n\n  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);\n\n  /* 4. Evaluate signal */\n  const result = evaluateSignal(closes, params);\n\n  if (result.signal === \'HOLD\') {\n    return json({ signal: \'HOLD\', ...result, mode: useTestnet ? \'testnet\' : \'real\', symbol: params.symbol });\n  }\n\n  /* 5. Place order */\n  const side = result.signal; // \'BUY\' | \'SELL\'\n  const qty = calcQuantity(result.price, effectiveSize, params.symbol);\n\n  let order: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;\n  let orderError: string | null = null;\n  try {\n    order = await signedPost(base, \'/api/v3/order\', settings.binance_api_key, settings.binance_api_secret, {\n      symbol: params.symbol.toUpperCase(),\n      side,\n      type: \'MARKET\',\n      quantity: String(qty),\n    });\n  } catch (e: unknown) {\n    orderError = (e as Error).message;\n  }\n\n  /* 6. Log trade to DB */\n  if (order) {\n    // Use TP1 as primary take_profit for DB record; log multi-TP as metadata in reason\n    const tpLevels = [tp1, tp2, tp3].filter(Boolean);\n    const multiTpNote = tpLevels.length > 1\n      ? ` | TP levels: ${tpLevels.map((t, i) => `TP${i+1}=${t}%`).join(\', \')}`\n      : \'\';\n    await client.from(\'trades\').insert({\n      user_id: userId,\n      signal_id: null,\n      symbol: params.symbol,\n      direction: side === \'BUY\' ? \'buy\' : \'sell\',\n      entry_price: result.price,\n      quantity: qty,\n      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n      status: \'open\',\n      binance_order_id: String(order.orderId ?? \'\'),\n      opened_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n    });\n\n    /* 7. Log signal */\n    await client.from(\'signals\').insert({\n      user_id: userId,\n      strategy_id: body.strategyId,\n      symbol: params.symbol,\n      direction: side === \'BUY\' ? \'buy\' : \'sell\',\n      confidence: 85,\n      entry_price: result.price,\n      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n      timeframe: effectiveTF,\n      reason: result.reason + multiTpNote,\n      status: \'executed\',\n    });\n  }\n\n  return json({\n    signal: result.signal,\n    reason: result.reason,\n    rsi: result.rsi,\n    ema_fast: result.ema_fast,\n    ema_slow: result.ema_slow,\n    price: result.price,\n    quantity: qty,\n    symbol: params.symbol,\n    sl: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n    tp1: tp1 ? result.price * (1 + tp1 / 100) : result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n    tp2: tp2 ? result.price * (1 + tp2 / 100) : null,\n    tp3: tp3 ? result.price * (1 + tp3 / 100) : null,\n    tp1Size, tp2Size, tp3Size,\n    mode: useTestnet ? \'testnet\' : \'real\',\n    order: order ?? null,\n    orderError,\n  });\n});\n\nfunction json(data: unknown, status = 200) {\n  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {\n    status,\n    headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n  });\n}\n'}]}

    49 /* ─── Binance helpers ─── */
    50 async function hmacSha256(secret: string, msg: string): Promise<string> {
    51   const enc = new TextEncoder();
    52   const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey('raw', enc.encode(secret), { name: 'HMAC', hash: 'SHA-256' }, false, ['sign']);
    53   const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign('HMAC', key, enc.encode(msg));
    54   return Array.from(new Uint8Array(sig)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
    55 }

    71 async function fetchKlines(base: string, symbol: string, interval: string, limit: number): Promise<OHLCV[]> {
    72   const url = `${base}/api/v3/klines?symbol=${symbol.toUpperCase()}&interval=${interval}&limit=${limit}`;
    73   const res = await fetch(url, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(10_000) });
    74   if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Klines fetch failed: ${res.status}`);
    75   const raw: unknown[][] = await res.json();
    76   return raw.map(c => ({
    77     close: parseFloat(c[4] as string),
    78     high: parseFloat(c[2] as string),
    79     low: parseFloat(c[3] as string),
    80   }));
    81 }
    82 
    83 /* ─── Technical Indicators ─── */
    84 function calcRSI(closes: number[], period: number): number {
    85   if (closes.length < period + 1) return 50;
    86   let gains = 0, losses = 0;
    87   for (let i = closes.length - period; i < closes.length; i++) {
    88     const diff = closes[i] - closes[i - 1];
    89     if (diff > 0) gains += diff; else losses -= diff;
    90   }
    91   const avgGain = gains / period;
    92   const avgLoss = losses / period;
    93   if (avgLoss === 0) return 100;
    94   const rs = avgGain / avgLoss;
    95   return +(100 - 100 / (1 + rs)).toFixed(2);
    96 }
    97 
    98 function calcEMA(closes: number[], period: number): number {
    99   if (closes.length < period) return closes[closes.length - 1];
   100   const k = 2 / (period + 1);
   101   let ema = closes.slice(0, period).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0) / period;
   102   for (let i = period; i < closes.length; i++) {
   103     ema = closes[i] * k + ema * (1 - k);
   104   }
   105   return +ema.toFixed(6);
   106 }
   107 
   108 /* ─── Signal evaluation ─── */
   109 function evaluateSignal(closes: number[], params: StrategyParams): SignalResult {
   110   const rsi = calcRSI(closes, params.rsi_length);
   111   const emaF = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_fast);
   112   const emaS = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_slow);
   113   const price = closes[closes.length - 1];
   114 
   115   const prevRsi = calcRSI(closes.slice(0, -1), params.rsi_length);
   116   const bullishCross = prevRsi <= params.oversold && rsi > params.oversold;
   117   const bearishCross = prevRsi >= params.overbought && rsi < params.overbought;
   118   const uptrend = emaF > emaS;
   119   const downtrend = emaF < emaS;
   120 
   121   const canLong = params.trade_direction === 'long' || params.trade_direction === 'both';
   122   const canShort = params.trade_direction === 'short' || params.trade_direction === 'both';
   123 
   124   if (canLong && bullishCross && uptrend) {
   125     return { signal: 'BUY', reason: `RSI crossed above oversold (${params.oversold}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} > EMA${params.ema_slow} uptrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };
   126   }
   127   if (canShort && bearishCross && downtrend) {
   128     return { signal: 'SELL', reason: `RSI crossed below overbought (${params.overbought}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} < EMA${params.ema_slow} downtrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };
   129   }
   130 
   131   return {
   132     signal: 'HOLD',
   133     reason: `RSI=${rsi} | EMA${params.ema_fast}=${emaF.toFixed(2)} | EMA${params.ema_slow}=${emaS.toFixed(2)} — no entry condition met`,
   134     rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price,
   135   };
   136 }
   137 
   138 /* ─── Minimum notional helper (USDT pairs) ─── */
   139 function calcQuantity(price: number, positionPct: number, _symbol: string): number {
   140   const budget = 1000 * (positionPct / 100); // assume $1000 base (real: fetch account balance)
   141   const qty = budget / price;
   142   // round to reasonable precision
   143   if (price > 1000) return +qty.toFixed(5);
   144   if (price > 1) return +qty.toFixed(3);
   145   return +qty.toFixed(1);
   146 }
   147

   151 };

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-ckp4ck3tg3r5/supabase/functions/bot-runner/index.ts]
Thought: 
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
import { createClient } from 'npm:@supabase/supabase-js@2';

/** Bot Runner — called every minute by pg_cron.
 *  Finds all active strategies whose timeframe interval has elapsed since last_executed_at
 *  and runs the strategy logic (same as execute-strategy) for each.
 */

const BINANCE_BASE_REAL = 'https://api.binance.com';
const BINANCE_BASE_TEST = 'https://testnet.binance.vision';
const RECV_WINDOW = '5000';

const corsHeaders = {
  'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type',
};

interface StrategyParams {
  rsi_length: number; overbought: number; oversold: number;
  ema_fast: number; ema_slow: number;
  symbol: string; timeframe: string;
  trade_direction: 'long' | 'short' | 'both';
}
interface OHLCV { close: number; high: number; low: number; }
interface SignalResult { signal: 'BUY'|'SELL'|'HOLD'; reason: string; rsi: number; ema_fast: number; ema_slow: number; price: number; }

/** Timeframe → milliseconds */
const TF_MS: Record<string, number> = {
  '1m': 60_000, '5m': 300_000, '15m': 900_000, '30m': 1_800_000,
  '1h': 3_600_000, '4h': 14_400_000, '1d': 86_400_000,
};
const TF_INTERVAL: Record<string, string> = {
  '1m':'1m','5m':'5m','15m':'15m','30m':'30m','1h':'1h','4h':'4h','1d':'1d',
};

function sb() {
  return createClient(Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!, Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!);
}

async function hmacSha256(secret: string, msg: string): Promise<string> {
  const enc = new TextEncoder();
  const key = await crypto.subtle.importKey('raw', enc.encode(secret), { name:'HMAC', hash:'SHA-256' }, false, ['sign']);
  const sig = await crypto.subtle.sign('HMAC', key, enc.encode(msg));
  return Array.from(new Uint8Array(sig)).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2,'0')).join('');
}

async function signedPost(base: string, path: string, apiKey: string, secret: string, params: Record<string,string>) {
  const ts = Date.now().toString();
  const all = { ...params, recvWindow: RECV_WINDOW, timestamp: ts };
  const qs = new URLSearchParams(all).toString();
  const sig = await hmacSha256(secret, qs);
  const res = await fetch(`${base}${path}?${qs}&signature=${sig}`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: { 'X-MBX-APIKEY': apiKey, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
  });
  const j = await res.json();
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(j.msg || `HTTP ${res.status}`);
  return j;
}

async function fetchKlines(base: string, symbol: string, interval: string, limit: number): Promise<OHLCV[]> {
  const url = `${base}/api/v3/klines?symbol=${symbol.toUpperCase()}&interval=${interval}&limit=${limit}`;
  const res = await fetch(url, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(10_000) });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Klines fetch failed: ${res.status}`);
  const raw: unknown[][] = await res.json();
  return raw.map(c => ({ close: parseFloat(c[4] as string), high: parseFloat(c[2] as string), low: parseFloat(c[3] as string) }));
}

function calcRSI(closes: number[], period: number): number {
  if (closes.length < period + 1) return 50;
  let gains = 0, losses = 0;
  for (let i = closes.length - period; i < closes.length; i++) {
    const diff = closes[i] - closes[i-1];
    if (diff > 0) gains += diff; else losses -= diff;
  }
  const avg = losses === 0 ? 100 : 100 - 100 / (1 + gains / losses);
  return +avg.toFixed(2);
}

function calcEMA(closes: number[], period: number): number {
  if (closes.length < period) return closes[closes.length - 1];
  const k = 2 / (period + 1);
  let ema = closes.slice(0, period).reduce((s,v) => s + v, 0) / period;
  for (let i = period; i < closes.length; i++) ema = closes[i] * k + ema * (1 - k);
  return +ema.toFixed(6);
}

function evaluateSignal(closes: number[], p: StrategyParams): SignalResult {
  const rsi = calcRSI(closes, p.rsi_length);
  const prevRsi = calcRSI(closes.slice(0,-1), p.rsi_length);
  const emaF = calcEMA(closes, p.ema_fast);
  const emaS = calcEMA(closes, p.ema_slow);
  const price = closes[closes.length - 1];
  const bullishCross = prevRsi <= p.oversold && rsi > p.oversold;
  const bearishCross = prevRsi >= p.overbought && rsi < p.overbought;
  const canLong = p.trade_direction === 'long' || p.trade_direction === 'both';
  const canShort = p.trade_direction === 'short' || p.trade_direction === 'both';
  if (canLong && bullishCross && emaF > emaS) return { signal:'BUY', reason:`RSI crossed above oversold(${p.oversold}) + uptrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast:emaF, ema_slow:emaS, price };
  if (canShort && bearishCross && emaF < emaS) return { signal:'SELL', reason:`RSI crossed below overbought(${p.overbought}) + downtrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast:emaF, ema_slow:emaS, price };
  return { signal:'HOLD', reason:`RSI=${rsi} | no entry condition met`, rsi, ema_fast:emaF, ema_slow:emaS, price };
}

function calcQty(price: number, pct: number): number {
  const budget = 1000 * (pct / 100);
  const qty = budget / price;
  if (price > 1000) return +qty.toFixed(5);
  if (price > 1) return +qty.toFixed(3);
  return +qty.toFixed(1);
}

Deno.serve(async (req) => {
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return new Response('ok', { headers: corsHeaders });

  const client = sb();
  const now = Date.now();
  const results: Array<{ strategyId: string; userId: string; signal: string; symbol: string; reason: string }> = [];

  try {
    // 1. Fetch all active strategies with analyzed params
    const { data: strategies, error } = await client
      .from('strategies')
      .select('*, user_id')
      .eq('status', 'active')
      .not('strategy_params', 'is', null);

    if (error) throw new Error(error.message);
    if (!strategies || strategies.length === 0) {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ran: 0, message: 'No active strategies' }), {
        headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      });
    }

    for (const strategy of strategies) {
      try {
        const params = strategy.strategy_params as StrategyParams;
        const tf = strategy.timeframe ?? params.timeframe ?? '1h';
        const intervalMs = TF_MS[tf] ?? TF_MS['1h'];

        // 2. Check if it's time to run (last_executed_at + interval <= now)
        const lastRan = strategy.last_executed_at ? new Date(strategy.last_executed_at).getTime() : 0;
        const nextRunAt = lastRan + intervalMs;
        if (now < nextRunAt) continue; // Not yet due — skip

        const userId: string = strategy.user_id;

        // 3. Load user settings
        const { data: settings } = await client
          .from('user_settings')
          .select('binance_api_key, binance_api_secret, use_testnet, bot_enabled, position_size_pct, stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct')
          .eq('user_id', userId)
          .maybeSingle();

        if (!settings?.binance_api_key || !settings?.binance_api_secret) continue;
        if (settings.bot_enabled === false) continue;

        const useTestnet: boolean = settings.use_testnet ?? true;
        const base = useTestnet ? BINANCE_BASE_TEST : BINANCE_BASE_REAL;

        // Risk priority: per-strategy > global
        const effectiveSL: number = strategy.stop_loss_pct ?? settings.stop_loss_pct ?? 2;
        const effectiveTP: number = strategy.tp1_pct ?? strategy.take_profit_pct ?? settings.take_profit_pct ?? 4;
        const effectiveSize: number = strategy.position_size_pct ?? settings.position_size_pct ?? 5;
        const tp1: number|null = strategy.tp1_pct ?? null;
        const tp2: number|null = strategy.tp2_pct ?? null;
        const tp3: number|null = strategy.tp3_pct ?? null;

        // 4. Fetch klines
        const interval = TF_INTERVAL[tf] ?? '1h';
        const klineLimit = Math.max(params.rsi_length + 10, params.ema_slow + 10, 60);
        const candles = await fetchKlines(base, params.symbol, interval, klineLimit);
        const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);

        // 5. Evaluate signal
        const result = evaluateSignal(closes, params);
        const ts = new Date().toISOString();

        // 6. Always update last_executed_at + last_signal
        await client.from('strategies').update({
          last_executed_at: ts,
          last_signal: result.signal,
        }).eq('id', strategy.id);

        results.push({ strategyId: strategy.id, userId, signal: result.signal, symbol: params.symbol, reason: result.reason });

        if (result.signal === 'HOLD') continue;

        // 7. Place order
        const side = result.signal as 'BUY' | 'SELL';
        const qty = calcQty(result.price, effectiveSize);
        let order: Record<string,unknown> | null = null;
        try {
          order = await signedPost(base, '/api/v3/order', settings.binance_api_key, settings.binance_api_secret, {
            symbol: params.symbol.toUpperCase(), side, type: 'MARKET', quantity: String(qty),
          });
        } catch (e) {
          console.error(`[bot-runner] Order failed for ${strategy.id}: ${(e as Error).message}`);
        }

        // 8. Log trade
        if (order) {
          const tpLevels = [tp1, tp2, tp3].filter(Boolean);
          const multiTpNote = tpLevels.length > 1
            ? ` | TP: ${tpLevels.map((t,i) => `TP${i+1}=${t}%`).join(', ')}`
            : '';
          await client.from('trades').insert({
            user_id: userId, signal_id: null, symbol: params.symbol,
            direction: side === 'BUY' ? 'buy' : 'sell',
            entry_price: result.price, quantity: qty,
            stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),
            take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),
            status: 'open', binance_order_id: String(order.orderId ?? ''), opened_at: ts,
          });
          await client.from('signals').insert({
            user_id: userId, strategy_id: strategy.id, symbol: params.symbol,
            direction: side === 'BUY' ? 'buy' : 'sell',
            confidence: 85, entry_price: result.price,
            stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),
            take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),
            timeframe: tf, reason: result.reason + multiTpNote, status: 'executed',
          });
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error(`[bot-runner] Error on strategy ${strategy.id}: ${(e as Error).message}`);
      }
    }

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ ran: results.length, results }), {
      headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  } catch (e) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: (e as Error).message }), {
      status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  }
});

```

ema_fast: number; ema_slow: number; price: number; }\n\n/** Timeframe → milliseconds */\nconst TF_MS: Record<string, number> = {\n  '1m': 60_000, '5m': 300_000, '15m': 900_000, '30m': 1_800_000,\n  '1h': 3_600_000, '4h': 14_400_000, '1d': 86_400_000,\n};\nconst TF_INTERVAL: Record<string, string> = {\n  '1m':'1m','5m':'5m','15m':'15m','30m':'30m','1h':'1h','4h':'4h','1d':'1d',\n};\n\nfunction evaluateSignal(closes: number[], params: StrategyParams): SignalResult {\n  const rsi = calcRSI(closes, params.rsi_length);\n  const emaF = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_fast);\n  const emaS = calcEMA(closes, params.ema_slow);\n  const price = closes[closes.length - 1];\n\n  const prevRsi = calcRSI(closes.slice(0, -1), params.rsi_length);\n  const bullishCross = prevRsi <= params.oversold && rsi > params.oversold;\n  const bearishCross = prevRsi >= params.overbought && rsi < params.overbought;\n  const uptrend = emaF > emaS;\n  const downtrend = emaF < emaS;\n\n  const canLong = params.trade_direction === \'long\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n  const canShort = params.trade_direction === \'short\' || params.trade_direction === \'both\';\n\n  if (canLong && bullishCross && uptrend) {\n    return { signal: \'BUY\', reason: `RSI crossed above oversold (${params.oversold}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} > EMA${params.ema_slow} uptrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n  if (canShort && bearishCross && downtrend) {\n    return { signal: \'SELL\', reason: `RSI crossed below overbought (${params.overbought}) with EMA${params.ema_fast} < EMA${params.ema_slow} downtrend confirmed`, rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price };\n  }\n\n  return {\n    signal: \'HOLD\',\n    reason: `RSI=${rsi} | EMA${params.ema_fast}=${emaF.toFixed(2)} | EMA${params.ema_slow}=${emaS.toFixed(2)} — no entry condition met`,\n    rsi, ema_fast: emaF, ema_slow: emaS, price,\n  };\n}\n\n/* ─── Minimum notional helper (USDT pairs) ─── */\nfunction calcQuantity(price: number, positionPct: number, _symbol: string): number {\n  const budget = 1000 * (positionPct / 100); // assume $1000 base (real: fetch account balance)\n  const qty = budget / price;\n  // round to reasonable precision\n  if (price > 1000) return +qty.toFixed(5);\n  if (price > 1) return +qty.toFixed(3);\n  return +qty.toFixed(1);\n}\n\nconst TF_INTERVAL: Record<string, string> = {\n  \'1m\': \'1m\', \'5m\': \'5m\', \'15m\': \'15m\', \'30m\': \'30m\',\n  \'1h\': \'1h\', \'4h\': \'4h\', \'1d\': \'1d\',\n};\n\n/* ─── Main handler ─── */\nDeno.serve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === \'OPTIONS\') return new Response(\'ok\', { headers: corsHeaders });\n\n  const authHeader = req.headers.get(\'authorization\') || \'\';\n  const token = authHeader.replace(\'Bearer \', \'\');\n  if (!token) return json({ error: \'Missing authorization\' }, 401);\n\n  let userId = \'\';\n  try {\n    const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split(\'.\')[1]));\n    userId = payload.sub;\n  } catch {\n    return json({ error: \'Invalid token\' }, 401);\n  }\n\n  let body: { strategyId: string };\n  try { body = await req.json(); } catch { return json({ error: \'Invalid JSON\' }, 400); }\n  if (!body.strategyId) return json({ error: \'strategyId is required\' }, 400);\n\n  const client = sb();\n\n  /* 1. Load strategy */\n  const { data: strategy, error: stratErr } = await client\n    .from(\'strategies\')\n    .select(\'*\')\n    .eq(\'id\', body.strategyId)\n    .eq(\'user_id\', userId)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (stratErr || !strategy) return json({ error: \'Strategy not found\' }, 404);\n\n  const params = strategy.strategy_params as StrategyParams | null;\n  if (!params) return json({ error: \'Strategy not analyzed yet. Click "AI Analyze" first.\' }, 400);\n\n  /* 2. Load user settings (API keys + risk params + testnet flag) */\n  const { data: settings } = await client\n    .from(\'user_settings\')\n    .select(\'binance_api_key, binance_api_secret, use_testnet, bot_enabled, position_size_pct, stop_loss_pct, take_profit_pct, min_confidence\')\n    .eq(\'user_id\', userId)\n    .maybeSingle();\n\n  if (!settings?.binance_api_key || !settings?.binance_api_secret) {\n    return json({ error: \'Binance API keys not configured in Settings.\' }, 400);\n  }\n\n  const useTestnet: boolean = settings.use_testnet ?? true;\n  const base = useTestnet ? BINANCE_BASE_TEST : BINANCE_BASE_REAL;\n\n  // Priority: per-strategy values > global user_settings fallback\n  const effectiveSL: number = (strategy.stop_loss_pct ?? settings.stop_loss_pct ?? 2);\n  const effectiveTP: number = (strategy.tp1_pct ?? strategy.take_profit_pct ?? settings.take_profit_pct ?? 4);\n  const effectiveSize: number = (strategy.position_size_pct ?? settings.position_size_pct ?? 5);\n  // Multi-TP levels (null = not configured)\n  const tp1: number | null = strategy.tp1_pct ?? null;\n  const tp2: number | null = strategy.tp2_pct ?? null;\n  const tp3: number | null = strategy.tp3_pct ?? null;\n  const tp1Size: number = strategy.tp1_size_pct ?? 33;\n  const tp2Size: number = strategy.tp2_size_pct ?? 33;\n  const tp3Size: number = strategy.tp3_size_pct ?? 34;\n\n  /* 3. Fetch live klines — strategy.timeframe top-level takes priority over strategy_params.timeframe */\n  const effectiveTF: string = (strategy.timeframe ?? params.timeframe ?? \'1h\');\n  const interval = TF_INTERVAL[effectiveTF] ?? \'1h\';\n  const klineLimit = Math.max(params.rsi_length + 10, params.ema_slow + 10, 60);\n  let candles: OHLCV[];\n  try {\n    candles = await fetchKlines(base, params.symbol, interval, klineLimit);\n  } catch (e: unknown) {\n    return json({ error: `Binance klines error: ${(e as Error).message}` }, 502);\n  }\n\n  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);\n\n  /* 4. Evaluate signal */\n  const result = evaluateSignal(closes, params);\n\n  if (result.signal === \'HOLD\') {\n    return json({ signal: \'HOLD\', ...result, mode: useTestnet ? \'testnet\' : \'real\', symbol: params.symbol });\n  }\n\n  /* 5. Place order */\n  const side = result.signal; // \'BUY\' | \'SELL\'\n  const qty = calcQuantity(result.price, effectiveSize, params.symbol);\n\n  let order: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;\n  let orderError: string | null = null;\n  try {\n    order = await signedPost(base, \'/api/v3/order\', settings.binance_api_key, settings.binance_api_secret, {\n      symbol: params.symbol.toUpperCase(),\n      side,\n      type: \'MARKET\',\n      quantity: String(qty),\n    });\n  } catch (e: unknown) {\n    orderError = (e as Error).message;\n  }\n\n  /* 6. Log trade to DB */\n  const now = new Date().toISOString();\n  if (order) {\n    // Use TP1 as primary take_profit for DB record; log multi-TP as metadata in reason\n    const tpLevels = [tp1, tp2, tp3].filter(Boolean);\n    const multiTpNote = tpLevels.length > 1\n      ? ` | TP levels: ${tpLevels.map((t, i) => `TP${i+1}=${t}%`).join(\', \')}`\n      : \'\';\n    await client.from(\'trades\').insert({\n      user_id: userId,\n      signal_id: null,\n      symbol: params.symbol,\n      direction: side === \'BUY\' ? \'buy\' : \'sell\',\n      entry_price: result.price,\n      quantity: qty,\n      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n      status: \'open\',\n      binance_order_id: String(order.orderId ?? \'\'),\n      opened_at: now,\n    });\n\n    /* 7. Log signal */\n    await client.from(\'signals\').insert({\n      user_id: userId,\n      strategy_id: body.strategyId,\n      symbol: params.symbol,\n      direction: side === \'BUY\' ? \'buy\' : \'sell\',\n      confidence: 85,\n      entry_price: result.price,\n      stop_loss: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n      take_profit: result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n      timeframe: effectiveTF,\n      reason: result.reason + multiTpNote,\n      status: \'executed\',\n    });\n  }\n\n  /* 8. Always update last_executed_at + last_signal on strategy */\n  await client.from(\'strategies\').update({\n    last_executed_at: now,\n    last_signal: result.signal,\n  }).eq(\'id\', body.strategyId);\n\n  return json({\n    signal: result.signal,\n    reason: result.reason,\n    rsi: result.rsi,\n    ema_fast: result.ema_fast,\n    ema_slow: result.ema_slow,\n    price: result.price,\n    quantity: qty,\n    symbol: params.symbol,\n    sl: result.price * (1 - effectiveSL / 100),\n    tp1: tp1 ? result.price * (1 + tp1 / 100) : result.price * (1 + effectiveTP / 100),\n    tp2: tp2 ? result.price * (1 + tp2 / 100) : null,\n    tp3: tp3 ? result.price * (1 + tp3 / 100) : null,\n    tp1Size, tp2Size, tp3Size,\n    mode: useTestnet ? \'testnet\' : \'real\',\n    order: order ?? null,\n    orderError,\n  });\n});\n\nfunction json(data: unknown, status = 200) {\n  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {\n    status,\n    headers: { ...corsHeaders, \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n  });\n}\n'}]}

New String: ```
  // ── Bot status helpers ──
  const TF_MS: Record<string, number> = {
    '1m': 60_000, '5m': 300_000, '15m': 900_000, '30m': 1_800_000,
    '1h': 3_600_000, '4h': 14_400_000, '1d': 86_400_000,
  };

  const getNextRunLabel = (strategy: Strategy): string => {
    const tf = strategy.timeframe ?? strategy.strategy_params?.timeframe ?? '1h';
    const intervalMs = TF_MS[tf] ?? TF_MS['1h'];
    const lastRan = strategy.last_executed_at ? new Date(strategy.last_executed_at).getTime() : 0;
    const nextAt = lastRan + intervalMs;
    const diffMs = nextAt - Date.now();
    if (diffMs <= 0) return 'Due now';
    const mins = Math.floor(diffMs / 60_000);
    const secs = Math.floor((diffMs % 60_000) / 1000);
    if (mins >= 60) return `${Math.floor(mins / 60)}h ${mins % 60}m`;
    if (mins > 0) return `${mins}m ${secs}s`;
    return `${secs}s`;
  };

  const getLastRunLabel = (ts: string | null): string => {
    if (!ts) return 'Never';
    const diff = Math.floor((Date.now() - new Date(ts).getTime()) / 1000);
    if (diff < 60) return `${diff}s ago`;
    if (diff < 3600) return `${Math.floor(diff / 60)}m ago`;
    if (diff < 86400) return `${Math.floor(diff / 3600)}h ago`;
    return `${Math.floor(diff / 86400)}d ago`;
  };
```
